5 import play.api._

24 /**
25  * This Controller handles API Requests concerning events
26  */
27 class EventController @Inject()(cc: ControllerComponents,
28                                 protected val dbConfigProvider: DatabaseConfigProvider,
29                                 val silhouette: Silhouette[AuthEnv],
30                                 val organizerService: OrganizerService,
31                                 val userService: UserService,
32                                 eventService: EventService,
33                                 locationService: LocationService)
34     (implicit context: ExecutionContext)
35     extends AbstractController(cc)
36     with HasDatabaseConfigProvider[JdbcProfile]
37     with Util {
38 
39   val log = Logger("api.event")
40 
41   def getEvent(id: Int) = Action.async { implicit request: Request[AnyContent] =>
42     log.debug("Rest request to get event")
43 
44     val q = for(e <- EventTable.event if e.id === id.bind) yield e;
45 
46     db.run(q.detailed).map(x => x.headOption match {
47       case Some(r) => Ok(Json.toJson(r))
48       case _ => NotFound
49     })
50   }
51 
52   def searchEvents(search: Option[String], location: Option[Int], category: Option[Int],
53                    sort: Option[String], sortDir: Boolean, from: Option[Timestamp], to: Option[Timestamp]) = Action.async { implicit request: Request[AnyContent] =>
54     log.debug("Rest request to search events")
55 
56     val q = for {
57       e <- event if similar(e.name,search.getOrElse("").bind) || search.getOrElse("").bind === ""
58                  if e.categories.filter(_.id === category.getOrElse(-1)).exists || category.getOrElse(-1).bind === -1
59                  if e.locationId - location.getOrElse(-1).bind === 0 || location.getOrElse(-1).bind === -1
60                  if e.from >= from.getOrElse(new Timestamp(0,0,0,0,0,0,0)) && e.from <= to.getOrElse(new Timestamp(4000,0,0,0,0,0,0))
61     } yield e
62 
63     val s = q.sortColumn(sort,sortDir).queryPaged.detailed
64     returnPaged(s,q,db)
65   }
66 
67   def getNearby(id: Int) = Action.async { implicit request: Request[AnyContent] =>
68     log.debug("Rest request to get events nearby another event")
69 
70     val q = for(e <- EventTable.event if e.id === id.bind) yield e;
71 
72     db.run(q.detailed).map(_.headOption).flatMap {
73       case Some(e) => {
74         val q = EventTable.event.join(LocationTable.location).on(_.locationId === _.id)
75           .sortBy(y => geoDistance(e.location.latitude, e.location.longitude, y._2.latitude, y._2.longitude))
76           .map(_._1).filter(y => y.id =!= e.id && y.from >= currentTimestamp)
77         val s = q.queryPaged.detailed
78         returnPaged(s,q,db)
79       }
80       case None => Future(NotFound)
81     }
82   }
83 
84   def getSameViewed(id: Int) = Action.async { implicit request: Request[AnyContent] =>
85     log.debug("Rest request to get events other participants also visit")
86 
87     val q = ParticipantCountView.participantCount.filter(_.id === id.bind)
88       .join(EventTable.event).on(_.event_fk === _.id)
89       .sortBy(y => y._1.count.desc).map(_._2)
90       .filter(y => y.id =!= id.bind && y.from >= currentTimestamp)
91 
92     val s = q.queryPaged.detailed
93 
94     returnPaged(s,q,db)
95   }
96 
97   def deleteEvent(id: Int) = organizerRequest(parse.default) { (request,organizer) =>
98     log.debug("Rest request to get event")
99 
100     val q = event.filter(x => x.id === id.bind && x.creatorId === organizer.id).delete
101 
102     db.run(q).map {
103       case 0 => NotFound
104       case x => Ok(Json.toJson(x))
105     }
106   }
107 
108   def createEvent() = organizerRequest(parse.json) { case (request,organizer) =>
109     EventForm.form.bindFromRequest()(request).fold(
110       form => {
111         Future.successful(BadRequest(Json.toJson(form.errors)))
112       },
113       data => {
114         log.debug("Rest request to create event")
115 
116         val location = locationService.insertOrGet(data.location)
117 
118         val imagesQuery = DBIO.sequence(data.images.map(x => ImageTable.image.filter(_.id === x.id.bind).result.map(l => l.map(r => (r,x.tag))))).map(_.flatten)
119 
120         val categoriesQuery = DBIO.sequence(
121           data.categories.map {
122             case cat =>
123               cat.id match {
124                 case None => insertAndReturn[Category,CategoryTable](CategoryTable.category,cat).map(x => List(x).seq)
125                 case Some(id) => CategoryTable.category.filter(_.id === id.bind).result
126               }
127           }).map(_.flatten)
128 
129         db.run(imagesQuery.zip(categoriesQuery)).zip(location).flatMap {
130           case ((images,categories),Some(location)) => {
131             val event = Event(None, data.name, data.from, data.to,
132                               data.description, data.shortDescription,
133                               organizer.id, location.id.getOrElse(-1),
134                               data.priceMin, data.priceMax)
135             db.run(insertAndReturn[Event,EventTable](EventTable.event,event)).map(r => (r,images,categories))
136           }.flatMap { case (event,images,categories) =>
137               val imagesAdd = ImageEntityTable.imageEntity ++= images.map(img => ImageEntity(img._1.id.getOrElse(-1),event.id.getOrElse(-1),EntityType.Event,img._2))
138               val categoriesAdd = EventCategoryTable.eventCategory ++= categories.map(cat => (cat.id.getOrElse(-1),event.id.getOrElse(-1)))
139               val eventDetailed = EventTable.event.filter(_.id === event.id.getOrElse(-1)).detailed
140               db.run(imagesAdd.zip(categoriesAdd) >> eventDetailed)
141           }.map(x => Ok(Json.toJson(x.head)))
142           case _ => Future.successful(BadRequest)
143         }
144       })
145   }
146 
147   def updateEvent(id: Int) = organizerRequest(parse.json) { case (request,organizer) =>
148     EventForm.form.bindFromRequest()(request).fold(
149       form => {
150         Future.successful(BadRequest(Json.toJson(form.errors)))
151       },
152       data => {
153         log.debug("Rest request to update event")
154 
155         val location = locationService.insertOrGet(data.location)
156 
157         val imagesQuery = DBIO.sequence(data.images.map(x => ImageTable.image.filter(_.id === x.id.bind).result.map(l => l.map(r => (r,x.tag))))).map(_.flatten)
158 
159         val categoriesQuery = DBIO.sequence(
160           data.categories.map {
161             case cat =>
162               cat.id match {
163                 case None => insertAndReturn[Category,CategoryTable](CategoryTable.category,cat).map(x => List(x).seq)
164                 case Some(id) => CategoryTable.category.filter(_.id === id.bind).result
165               }
166           }).map(_.flatten)
167 
168         val eventQuery = EventTable.event.filter(x => x.id === id.bind && x.creatorId === organizer.id).result.map(_.headOption)
169 
170         db.run(imagesQuery.zip(categoriesQuery).zip(eventQuery)).zip(location).flatMap {
171           case (((images,categories),Some(event)),Some(location)) => {
172             val event = Event(Some(id), data.name, data.from, data.to,
173                               data.description, data.shortDescription,
174                               organizer.id, location.id.getOrElse(-1),
175                               data.priceMin, data.priceMax)
176 
177             val getQuery = EventTable.event.filter(x => x.id === id.bind && x.creatorId === organizer.id)
178 
179             db.run(getQuery.update(event) >> getQuery.result.map(_.head))
180               .map(r => Some((r,images,categories)))
181           }
182           case _ => Future.successful(None)
183         }.flatMap {
184           case Some((event,images,categories)) => {
185             val dropImages = ImageEntityTable.imageEntity.filter(x => x.entityId === id && x.entityType === EntityType.Event).delete
186             val dropCategories = EventCategoryTable.eventCategory.filter(x => x.eventID === id).delete
187             val dropQuery = dropImages.zip(dropCategories)
188 
189             val imagesAdd = ImageEntityTable.imageEntity ++= images.map(img => ImageEntity(img._1.id.getOrElse(-1),event.id.getOrElse(-1),EntityType.Event, img._2))
190             val categoriesAdd = EventCategoryTable.eventCategory ++= categories.map(cat => (cat.id.getOrElse(-1),event.id.getOrElse(-1)))
191             val eventDetailed = EventTable.event.filter(_.id === event.id.getOrElse(-1)).detailed
192             db.run(dropQuery >> imagesAdd.zip(categoriesAdd) >> eventDetailed).map(x => Some(x))
193           }
194           case None => Future.successful(None)
195         }.map {
196           case Some(e) => Ok(Json.toJson(e))
197           case None => BadRequest
198         }
199       })
200   }
201 
202   def insertCSV = organizerRequest(parse.multipartFormData) { case (request,organizer) =>
203     log.debug("Rest request to insert events by csv")
204 
205     request.body.file("csv").map { case x =>
206       val file = x.ref.path.toFile()
207 
208       eventService.insertCSV(file,organizer)
209      }.map(_.map(x => Ok(Json.toJson(x)))).headOption.getOrElse(Future.successful(BadRequest))
210   }
211 
212   def participate(id: Int) = userRequest(parse.default) { case (request,user) =>
213     log.debug("Rest request to participate in event")
214 
215     val q = (event.filter(x => x.id === id.bind).result)
216       .zip(ParticipantTable.participant.filter(x => x.eventID === id.bind && x.userID === user.id.getOrElse(-1).bind).result)
217 
218     db.run(q).map(x => (x._1.headOption,x._2.headOption)).flatMap {
219       case (Some(e),None) => {
220         db.run(ParticipantTable.participant += ((user.id.getOrElse(-1),id)))
221         Future.successful(Ok)
222       }
223       case (Some(e),Some(p)) => Future.successful(Conflict)
224       case (None,_) => Future.successful(BadRequest)
225     }
226   }
227 
228   def unparticipate(id: Int) = userRequest(parse.default) { case (request,user) =>
229     log.debug("Rest request to unparticipate in event")
230 
231     db.run(ParticipantTable.participant.filter(x => x.eventID === id.bind && x.userID === user.id.getOrElse(-1).bind).delete)
232       .flatMap {
233       case 1 => {
234         Future.successful(Ok)
235       }
236       case _ => Future.successful(BadRequest)
237     }
238   }
